ÿ¥ÿÆÿµŸä","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Uno Classic is a fast and frenzied card game has been a family favorite for over four decades now. Featuring a balanced mix of gentle strategy and chance, it‚Äôs entertaining for all ages and can be played anywhere.\r\n\r\nIt is a pretty popular game, and for a good reason: it's a game that's very simple to learn, but still has some strategic complexity. It's on the shallow end of complexity. \r\n\r\nThe objective of the game is to get rid of your cards fast to win this game! \r\n\r\nBut Uno Classic game not just a feast of fun ‚Äì it also helps develop kids counting, matching, critical thinking, and social interaction.\r\n\r\nUno is a simple color and number matching game. The deck consists of 108 cards, of which there are 25 of each color (red, green, blue, and yellow), each color having two of each rank except zero. The ranks in each color are zero to nine, \"Skip\", \"Draw Two\", and \"Reverse\" (the last three being \"action cards\"). In addition, the deck contains four each of \"Wild\" and \"Wild Draw Four\" cards\r\n\r\nEach player is dealt 7 cards and the remaining cards are placed face down to form a draw pile. \r\nThe first player has to match the card in the discard pile either by number or color or the player can throw down a Wild Card else he must pick a card from the draw pile.
